## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Created: __init__()
    Created --> Modified: setter called
    Modified --> Modified: setter called
    Modified --> Validated: validate()
    Validated --> [*]
    
    state Modified {
        [*] --> CheckValue
        CheckValue --> AssertType
        AssertType --> CompareValue
        CompareValue --> UpdateField: value changed
        CompareValue --> [*]: value unchanged
        UpdateField --> AddDirtyField
        AddDirtyField --> [*]
    }
```
